**GT expression simplified:**
```
0.11424*(1 - P/40.698)*P + 0.11424*(1 - exp(-0.08368*P))*P + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

Expanding:
```
0.11424*P - 0.11424*P²/40.698 + 0.11424*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

Combining:
```
-0.002807*P² + 0.22848*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

The GT has these structural components:
1. A `P²` term
2. A `P` term  
3. A `P*exp(-αP)` term (interaction between P and exponential of P)
4. A `P*exp(-βt)` term (interaction between P and exponential of t)

The key challenging terms are `P*exp(-0.08368*P)` and `P*exp(-0.08368*t)`.

Let me check candidates with `exp` terms involving P:

**Candidate 31:** `P*c0 + c1*t + c2 + c3*log(c4*exp(P*c5) + 1)`

When `c4*exp(P*c5)` is large, `log(c4*exp(P*c5)+1) ≈ log(c4) + P*c5`, which is linear in P. When `c4` is small, `log(c4*exp(P*c5)+1) ≈ c4*exp(P*c5)`. But this doesn't have P*exp(P) structure and no t-dependent exponential.

**Candidate 33:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2/(P+c3) + c4t + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(P*c8)+1)`
Similar issue - no `P*exp(-βt)` term.

**Candidate 39:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + P^c2*c3 + c4t + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(Pc8 + c9*t) + 1)`
This has `log(c7*exp(Pc8 + c9*t) + 1)`. If c7 is small, this ≈ `c7*exp(Pc8 + c9*t)` = `c7*exp(c8*P)*exp(c9*t)`. But we need separate terms `P*exp(αP)` and `P*exp(βt)`, not a product `exp(αP + βt)`.

**Candidate 49:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2*exp(c3*t) + c4*tanh(c5*t+c6) + c7 + c8*t`
This has `P*exp(c3*t)` which matches the `P*exp(-βt)` term! But we also need `P*exp(-αP)`. The `tanh` term can't produce that.

**Candidate 38:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + P^c2*c3 + c4t + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(Pc8) + 1)`
If c7 is small: `c6*c7*exp(Pc8)`. With `P^c2*c3` setting c2=1 gives Pc3. No `P*exp(βt)` term.

None of the candidates simultaneously have:
- `P*exp(αP)` structure
- `P*exp(βt)` structure

The GT requires both an exponential in P multiplied by P AND an exponential in t multiplied by P. Looking through all 50 candidates, none have both `P*exp(something*P)` and `P*exp(something*t)` (or equivalent structures).

Some candidates have exponential-like terms in t (like `exp(c/(c+t))`) but these produce `exp(c/t)` type behavior, not `exp(-ct)`.

Candidate 49 has `P*exp(c3*t)` matching one term, but lacks `P*exp(c*P)`.

No candidate captures both essential nonlinear structures simultaneously.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG14)

GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*(c4 - exp(-c5*P))*P + c6*P*exp(-c7*t)

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) and compare each candidate to it.

## Ground Truth Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.11424*(1 - P/40.698)*P + 0.11424*(1 - exp(-0.08368*P))*P + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

Let me expand this:
```
0.11424*P - 0.11424*P²/40.698 + 0.11424*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

Simplifying:
```
-0.002807*P² + 0.22848*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

The GT has these basis functions:
1. **P²** (quadratic in P)
2. **P** (linear in P)
3. **P·exp(-c·P)** (P times exponential in P)
4. **P·exp(-c·t)** (P times exponential in t)

The key structural features are:
- A term involving `P*exp(αP)` where α is negative
- A term involving `P*exp(βt)` where β is negative
- Polynomial terms in P (P² and P)
- The t-dependence comes ONLY through `P*exp(-c*t)` — this couples P and t

Let me now check each candidate. I need to find candidates that can reproduce all four basis functions.

### Critical observations about the t-dependence:
The GT has `P*exp(-0.08368*t)` as the t-dependent term. This means the t-dependence is coupled with P. Any candidate that has t-dependence NOT coupled with P (like standalone `c*t`, `c*t²`, `log(t+1)`, `exp(c/t)`, `sin(t)`, `tanh(t)`, etc.) cannot match unless those terms can be zeroed out AND the candidate also has a `P*exp(-ct)` type term.

### Candidate-by-candidate analysis:

**Candidate 1:** `P²*c0/(c1+t²) + P²*c2 + P*c3 + c4*t/(c1+t²) + c5*exp(c6/(c7+t)) + c8*t + c9*t²`
- No P*exp(cP) term. No P*exp(ct) term. The exp term is `exp(c/(c+t))` which is not `P*exp(-ct)`.
- Missing basis functions. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 2:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2*c3*t^c4 + c5*exp(c6/(c7+t)) + c8*t + c9*t²`
- Has `P^c2*t^c4` — this is a power-law coupling, not exponential.
- No P*exp(cP) term. No P*exp(ct) term.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 3:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(1+c3/P) + P^c4*c5*t^c6 + c7*log(c8*t+1)`
- `P*log(1+c3/P)`: For large P, this ≈ c3, for small P this diverges. Not equivalent to P*exp(cP).
- No P*exp(ct) term.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 4:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2*c3*t^c4 + c5*t*exp(c6*t) + c7*t/P^5`
- No P*exp(cP) term. `t*exp(c*t)` ≠ `P*exp(-ct)`.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 5:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*sin(c3*t+c4) + P*c5*log(P*c6+1) + c7*exp(c8/(c9+t))`
- Has `P*sin(c3*t+c4)`: This oscillates in t, while GT has `P*exp(-ct)` which decays. Not equivalent.
- `P*log(P*c6+1)` ≠ `P*exp(cP)`.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 6:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*t + c3 + c4*log(P*c5*t+1) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*t+1)+c9)`
- `log(P*c5*t+1)` couples P and t but not in the right way.
- No P*exp(cP) or P*exp(ct) terms.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 7:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*log(c3*t+1) + c4*log(c5*exp(P*c6)+1)`
- `log(c5*exp(Pc6)+1)`: For large Pc6, this ≈ Pc6 + log(c5). For small Pc6, this ≈ log(c5+1). This is a softplus-like function in P, not P*exp(cP).
- `log(c3*t+1)` ≠ `P*exp(-ct)`.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 8:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2*c3 + c4*t + c5 + c6*t²`
- No t-P coupling. No exp terms at all.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 9:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + P*c4*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7*t + c8`
- `P*sin(c5*t+c6)` oscillates, not exponential decay.
- `P*log(Pc3+1)` ≠ `P*exp(cP)`.

**Candidate 10:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*t + c3 + c4*t² + c5*exp(c6/(c7+t))`

- No P*exp(ct) coupling.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 25:** `P*c0 + c1*t + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(P*c5+1)+c6)`
- Too simple. No P² term, no exp terms.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 26:** `P²*c0 + P²*c1/(P+c2) + P*c3 + c4*t + c5 + c6*exp(P*c7)`
- `c6*exp(Pc7)`: This is exp(cP), not P*exp(cP). These are different functions.
- No P*exp(ct) coupling.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 27:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*exp(c3/(c4+t)) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*t+1)+c8) + c9/P^5`
- No P*exp(cP). No P*exp(ct).
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 28:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*log(c3*t+1) + c4*exp(c5/(c6+t)) + c7*t + c8/(P+c9)`
- No P*exp(cP). No P*exp(ct).
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 29:** `P²*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2 + c3*exp(c4/(c5+t)) + c6*t + c7*exp(P^c8*c9)`
- `exp(P^c8*c9)`: If c8=1, this is exp(c9*P), not P*exp(cP).
- No P*exp(ct).
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 30:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(P*c3+1) + c4*t + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*t+1)+c9)`
- sin(log(t)) for t-dependence, not P*exp(-ct).
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 31:** `P*c0 + c1*t + c2 + c3*log(c4*exp(P*c5)+1)`
- `log(c4*exp(Pc5)+1)` = softplus-like. For large Pc5: ≈ Pc5 + log(c4). Not P*exp(cP).
- No P*exp(ct).
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 32:** `P²*c0 + P²*c1/(P+c2) + P²*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5/(P+c6)² + P*c7 + c8*t + c9`
- All rational in P, linear in t. No exp terms.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 33:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2/(P+c3) + c4*t + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(P*c8)+1)`
- `log(c7*exp(Pc8)+1)`: softplus, not P*exp(cP).
- No P*exp(ct).
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 34:** `P*c0 + P^c1*c2 + c3*t + c4`
- Too simple. No exp terms.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 35:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*tanh(c3*t+c4) + c5*exp(c6/(c7+t))`
- tanh for t, not P*exp(-ct). No P*exp(cP).
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 36-50:** Let me continue checking for the key features: P*exp(cP) and P*exp(ct).

**Candidate 36:** No P*exp(cP) or P*exp(ct). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 37:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5/(c6+t))`
- `t*exp(c3*t)` not coupled with P. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 38:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2*c3 + c4*t + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(P*c8)+1)`
- Softplus, not P*exp(cP). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 39:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2*c3 + c4*t + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(P*c8+c9*t)+1)`
- `log(c7*exp(Pc8+c9t)+1)`: For large argument ≈ Pc8+c9t+log(c7). This couples P and t linearly, not as P*exp(-ct). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 40:** Same structure as 43 essentially. tanh, not exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 41:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(1+c3/P) + P*c4/(P+c5) + c6*t + c7 + c8/P^5 + c9*t/P^5`
- No exp terms. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 42:** No P*exp(cP) or P*exp(ct). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 43:** tanh, not exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 44:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*log(c3*t+1) + c4*exp(c5/(c6+t)) + c7*t`
- No P*exp(cP). No P*exp(ct). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 45:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2*c3 + P^c4*c5*t + c6*t + c7`
- Power laws, no exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 46:** Complex rational expression in t. No exp terms. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 47:** sin, no exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 48:** log, no exp coupling. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 49:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*tanh(c5*t+c6) + c7 + c8*t`
- Has `P*exp(c3*t)` — this matches the P*exp(-ct) term if c3 < 0!
- But needs P*exp(cP) for the other term, which is missing. tanh(c5*t+c6) cannot match P*exp(cP).
- Wait, let me reconsider. Can we set tanh terms to zero and check if remaining terms match GT?
- If we zero out tanh: `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c7 + c8*t`
- GT needs: P² + P + P*exp(cP) + P*exp(ct)
- This candidate has P*exp(ct) but not P*exp(cP). Missing basis function.
- **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 50:** Rational in t with fractional powers. No exp. **[NO MATCH]**

None of the candidates contain both `P*exp(c*P)` and `P*exp(c*t)` terms simultaneously, which are essential basis functions of the GT.
